href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/xengine-kit-xeg-spatialupscaledescription">XEG_SpatialUpscaleDescription</a></p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>此结构体描述下发空域GPU超分渲染命令时需要的图像信息。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>struct  <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/xengine-kit-xeg-temporalupscalecreateinfo">XEG_TemporalUpscaleCreateInfo</a></p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>此结构体描述创建<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/xengine-kit-xengine#xeg_temporalupscale">XEG_TemporalUpscale</a>对象的信息。当结构体中的信息变化时，需要创建新的<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/xengine-kit-xengine#xeg_temporalupscale">XEG_TemporalUpscale</a>对象。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>struct  <a width="50%"><p>此结构体描述下发时域AI超分渲染命令时的输入信息。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> </div> <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 2801px;"><h3 id="宏定义" </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/xengine-kit-xengine#xeg_adaptive_vrs_error_sensitivity">XEG_ADAPTIVE_VRS_ERROR_SENSITIVITY</a>   0x4U</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>用于设置<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/xengine-kit-xengine#hms_xeg_adaptivevrsparameter">HMS_XEG_AdaptiveVRSParameter</a>接口的ERROR_SENSITIVITY参数，表示控制生成着色率图像的阈值。该值越大，平均着色率越小，即性能会越好但画质会劣化。建议取值范围为[0, 1]。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/xengine-kit-xengine#xeg_adaptive_vrs_flip">XEG_ADAPTIVE_VRS_FLIP</a>   0x5U</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/xengine-kit-xengine#xeg_neural_upscale_sharpness">XEG_NEURAL_UPSCALE_SHARPNESS</a>   0x2U</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/xengine-kit-xengine#xeg_spatial_upscale_sharpness">XEG_SPATIAL_UPSCALE_SHARPNESS</a>   0x2U</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>用于设置<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/xengine-kit-xengine#hms_xeg_spatialupscaleparameter">HMS_XEG_SpatialUpscaleParameter</a>接口的SHARPNESS参数。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/xengine-kit-xengine#xeg_temporal_upscale_input_size">XEG_TEMPORAL_UPSCALE_INPUT_SIZE</a>   0x1U</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>用于通过<a width="50%"><p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/xengine-kit-xengine#xeg_temporal_upscale_jitter_num">XEG_TEMPORAL_UPSCALE_JITTER_NUM</a>   0x2U</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/xengine-kit-xengine#xeg_temporal_upscale_depth_reversed">XEG_TEMPORAL_UPSCALE_DEPTH_REVERSED</a>   0x3U</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>用于通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/xengine-kit-xengine#hms_xeg_temporalupscaleparameter">HMS_XEG_TemporalUpscaleParameter</a>接口设置是否存在深度反转。true表示存在深度反转，false表示不存在深度反转。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/xengine-kit-xengine#xeg_temporal_upscale_reset_history">XEG_TEMPORAL_UPSCALE_RESET_HISTORY</a>   0x4U</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>用于通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/xengine-kit-xengine#hms_xeg_temporalupscaleparameter">HMS_XEG_TemporalUpscaleParameter</a>接口设置是否重置历史帧数据，true表示重置，false表示不重置。在历史帧未使用超分，并且当前帧开始使用超分的情况下建议设置为true。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/xengine-kit-xengine#xeg_temporal_upscale_steady_level">XEG_TEMPORAL_UPSCALE_STEADY_LEVEL</a>   0x5U</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>用于通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/xengine-kit-xengine#hms_xeg_temporalupscaleparameter">HMS_XEG_TemporalUpscaleParameter</a>接口设置画面偏向当前帧（鬼影少但可能存在闪烁）还是历史帧（鬼影多但是更稳定）的平衡程度。取值范围为[0.0, 1.0]，值越大越偏向历史帧。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/xengine-kit-xengine#xeg_max_extension_name_size">XEG_MAX_EXTENSION_NAME_SIZE</a>   256</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>XEngine扩展特性名称支持的最大长度。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> </div> <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 5746px;"><h3 id="类型定义" device-type="phone,tablet,2in1">XEG_ADAPTIVE_VRS_ERROR_SENSITIVITY<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="xeg_adaptive_vrs_error_sensitivity" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="cpp prettyprint linenums hljs language-cpp" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-meta">#<span class="hljs-keyword">define</span> XEG_ADAPTIVE_VRS_ERROR_SENSITIVITY   0x4U</span></li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>用于设置<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/xengine-kit-xengine#hms_xeg_adaptivevrsparameter">HMS_XEG_AdaptiveVRSParameter</a>接口的ERROR_SENSITIVITY参数，表示控制生成着色率图像的阈值。该值越大，平均着色率越小，即性能会越好但画质会劣化。建议取值范围为[0, 1]。</p> <p>使用此宏定义时通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/xengine-kit-xengine#hms_xeg_adaptivevrsparameter">HMS_XEG_AdaptiveVRSParameter</a>接口设置ERROR_SENSITIVITY参数，向接口传递的param必须是GLfloat指针，否则将产生未定义行为，如渲染效果不正确或者程序崩溃。 可选参数，默认为0.5。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 5.0.0(12)</p> </div> <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 378px;"><h3 id="xeg_adaptive_vrs_extension_name" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="xeg_adaptive_vrs_flip" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="cpp prettyprint linenums hljs language-cpp" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-meta">#<span class="hljs-keyword">define</span> XEG_ADAPTIVE_VRS_FLIP   0x5U</span></li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>用于设置<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/xengine-kit-xengine#hms_xeg_adaptivevrsparameter">HMS_XEG_AdaptiveVRSParameter</a>接口的FLIP参数，该参数用于控制是否执行图像上下翻转。</p> <p>使用此宏定义时通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/xengine-kit-xengine#hms_xeg_adaptivevrsparameter">HMS_XEG_AdaptiveVRSParameter</a>接口设置FLIP参数，向接口传递的param必须是GLboolean指针，否则将产生未定义行为，如渲染效果不正确或者程序崩溃。 可选参数，默认为false。true表示执行上下翻转，false表示不执行上下翻转。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 5.0.0(12)</p> </div> <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 474px;"><h3 id="xeg_adaptive_vrs_input_region" device-type="phone,tablet,2in1">XEG_ADAPTIVE_VRS_INPUT_REGION<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="xeg_adaptive_vrs_input_region" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="cpp prettyprint linenums hljs language-cpp" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-meta">#<span class="hljs-keyword">define</span> XEG_ADAPTIVE_VRS_INPUT_REGION   0x2U</span></li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>用于设置<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/xengine-kit-xengine#hms_xeg_adaptivevrsparameter">HMS_XEG_AdaptiveVRSParameter</a>接口的INPUT_REGION参数，表示上一帧渲染管线最终渲染的图像区域。</p> <p>使用此宏定义时通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/xengine-kit-xengine#hms_xeg_adaptivevrsparameter">HMS_XEG_AdaptiveVRSParameter</a>接口设置INPUT_REGION参数，向接口传递的param必须是长度为4的GLuint类型数组，依次为渲染图像区域左下角的坐标和渲染图像区域的宽高，否则将产生未定义行为，如渲染效果不正确或者程序崩溃。 可选参数，默认为[0, 0, INPUT_SIZE[0], INPUT_SIZE[1]]。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 5.0.0(12)</p> </div> <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 474px;"><h3 id="xeg_adaptive_vrs_input_size" device-type="phone,tablet,2in1">XEG_ADAPTIVE_VRS_INPUT_SIZE<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="xeg_adaptive_vrs_input_size" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-meta">#<span class="hljs-keyword">define</span> XEG_NEURAL_UPSCALE_SCISSOR   0x1U</span></li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>用于通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/xengine-kit-xengine#hms_xeg_neuralupscaleparameter">HMS_XEG_NeuralUpscaleParameter</a>接口设置超分的裁剪窗口参数，裁剪窗口用于确定对输入图像采样的区域。</p> <p>使用此宏定义设置裁剪窗口参数时，向接口传递的param值必须是长度为4的无符号整数数组，否则将产生未定义行为，如渲染效果不正确或者程序崩溃。数组中的值依次为：x, y, width, height，其中x、y确定裁剪窗口的左下角，width、height分别确定裁剪窗口的宽和高。 可选参数，不设置裁剪窗口参数时的默认值为(0, 0, 输入纹理的宽, 输入纹理的高)。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 5.0.0(12)</p> </div> <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 450px;"><h3 id="xeg_neural_upscale_sharpness" active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-vab-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="cpp prettyprint linenums hljs language-cpp" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">typedef</span> <span class="hljs-title">void</span><span class="hljs-params">(GL_APIENTRYP  PFN_HMS_XEG_DISPATCHADAPTIVEVRS)</span> <span class="hljs-params">(GLfloat *reprojectionMatrix, GLuint inputColorImage, GLuint inputDepthImage, GLuint shadingRateImage)</span></span></li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>计算着色率图像的函数指针定义。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 5.0.0(12)</p> <p><strong>参数:</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.68.7.1.3.1.1" width="50%"><p>名称</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.68.7.1.3.1.2" width="50%"><p>描述</p> </th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>reprojectionMatrix</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>当前帧和上一帧进行计算的结果矩阵的指针，计算公式为：（上一帧投影矩阵* 上一帧的观察矩阵）* （（当前帧的投影矩阵* 当前帧的观察矩阵）的逆矩阵），矩阵必须是4*4列主序的矩阵。可选参数，非空时画质较优。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>inputColorImage</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>上一帧渲染管线最终渲染结果颜色附件纹理ID。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>inputDepthImage</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>当前帧渲染管线最终渲染结果深度附件纹理ID。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>shadingRateImage</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>用于生成着色率图信息的纹理ID，需用户创建并输入。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content"><p>纹理类型需要是GL_TEXTURE_2D且mipLevels为1。</p> </div></div></div> </div> <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 947px;"><h3 id="pfn_hms_xeg_enumeratedeviceextensionproperties" device-type="phone,tablet,2in1">PFN_HMS_XEG_EnumerateDeviceExtensionProperties<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" *pProperties)</span></span></li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>XEngine Vulkan扩展特性查询接口函数指针定义。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 5.0.0(12)</p> <p><strong>参数:</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.69.7.1.3.1.1" width="50%"><p>名称</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.69.7.1.3.1.2" width="50%"><p>描述</p> </th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>physicalDevice</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>当前使用的Vulkan物理设备。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>pPropertyCount</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>查询或传入扩展特性的数量，当<strong>pProperties</strong>为nullptr时返回当前支持的XEngine扩展特性数量。 当传入的<strong>propertyCount</strong>大于或等于真实支持的XEngine扩展特性数量时，通过<strong>pProperties</strong>返回查询信息，返回结果为VK_SUCCESS。 当传入的<strong>propertyCount</strong>小于真实支持的XEngine扩展特性数量时，通过<strong>pProperties</strong>返回查询信息，但返回结果为VK_INCOMPLETE。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>pProperties</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>查询到的XEngine扩展特性，通过结构体<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/xengine-kit-xeg-extensionproperties">XEG_ExtensionProperties</a>指针返回。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回：</strong></p> <p>返回VkResult类型错误码，查询成功时返回值为VK_SUCCESS。 当<strong>pProperties</strong>不为nullptr且传入的<strong>propertyCount</strong>小于实际支持的XEngine扩展特性数量时返回值为VK_INCOMPLETE，表示查询特性不完整。</p> </div> class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>物体的动态遮罩图像，格式需要是GL_RED或其兼容格式。R通道的合法值为0.0，0.2或1.0，其中0.0表示静态物体，0.2表示运动物体如人物，1.0表示特效或半透明物体。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>jitterX</p> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>pDescription</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>执行渲染命令的信息结构体的指针，若使用DDGI渲染，为结构体<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/xengine-kit-xeg-ddgidescription">XEG_DDGIDescription</a>的指针，若使用NNGI渲染，为结构体<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/xengine-kit-xeg-nngidescription">XEG_NNGIDescription</a>的指针，不允许为空。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回：</strong></p> <p>返回一个VkResult类型的错误码，返回值为VK_SUCCESS表示执行成功。</p> </div> <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 683px;"><h3 id="hms_xeg_cmdrenderrtreflection" href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/xengine-kit-xeg-temporalupscalecreateinfo">XEG_TemporalUpscaleCreateInfo</a>的指针，不允许为空。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>pTemporalUpscale</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>指向句柄的指针，创建的<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/xengine-kit-xengine#xeg_temporalupscale">XEG_TemporalUpscale</a>在此句柄中返回。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回：</strong></p> <p>返回一个VkResult类型的错误码，返回值为VK_SUCCESS表示执行成功。</p> </div> <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 549px;"><h3 id="hms_xeg_destroyadaptivevrs" )</span></span></li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>计算着色率图像。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 5.0.0(12)</p> <p><strong>参数:</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.130.7.1.3.1.1" width="50%"><p>名称</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.130.7.1.3.1.2" width="50%"><p>描述</p> </th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>reprojectionMatrix</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>执行时域AI超分渲染命令。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 6.0.0(20)</p> <p><strong>参数:</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> width="50%"><p>描述</p> </th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>inputTexture</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>超分输入纹理。输入纹理是GL_TEXTURE_2D类型且mipLevels为1，支持的最大尺寸为2048 * 1024。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>depthTexture</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>深度纹理。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>motionVectorTexture</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>运动矢量图像。运动矢量的计算方式为当前渲染像素的NDC坐标的XY值减去上一帧的NDC坐标的XY值。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>dynamicMaskTexture</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>物体的动态遮罩图像，格式需要是GL_RED或其兼容格式。R通道的合法值为0.0，0.2或1.0，其中0.0表示静态物体，0.2表示运动物体如人物，1.0表示特效或半透明物体。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>jitterX</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>相机在X方向上的抖动。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>jitterY</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>相机在Y方向上的抖动。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> </div> <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 652px;"><h3
